// AA // KK
when ( Hand = AA or Hand = KK or Hand = QQ or Hand = JJ or Hand = AK ) and TotalInvested > 100% StackSize RaiseMax Force
when ( Hand = AA or Hand = KK or Hand = QQ or Hand = JJ or Hand = AK ) and BigBlindSize <= 80 and StackSize < 12 RaiseMax Force
when OpponentsAtTable >= 6 and ( Hand = AA or Hand = KK ) and BetSize > 25% StackSize RaiseMax Force

when OpponentsAtTable >= 6 and ( Hand = AA or Hand = KK ) and Raises > 0 RaiseMax Force
